I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
RangeError: Position out of range when deleting after multi-column block
### What’s broken?

When using the multi-column feature, continuously pressing Backspace after typing in a block following a multi-column layout causes a runtime error:

```RangeError: Position X out of range```

This crashes the editor and breaks further interaction.

<img width="1225" height="838" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/de3d5796-0967-40e8-bbd3-98c4147efaec" />

<img width="592" height="174" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/3ccd0b6d-4eed-46c0-8193-34692e7e225f" />

### What did you expect to happen?

- Text should be deleted normally
- Editor should remain stable
- No runtime errors should occur


### Steps to reproduce

1. Insert a multi-column block (e.g., 3 columns)
2. Move cursor to the next block (below the columns)
3. Type some text (e.g., aaa)
4. Press and hold Backspace to delete continuously

### BlockNote version

"@blocknote/xl-multi-column": "0.47.1"

### Environment

Chrome

### Additional context

- This issue appears to be related to how the multi-column structure interacts with deletion logic.
- Likely caused by an invalid ProseMirror transaction when deleting across structural boundaries.
- Happens more frequently when holding down Backspace (rapid consecutive deletes).

### Contribution

- [ ] I'd be interested in contributing a fix for this issue

### Sponsor

- [ ] I'm a [sponsor](https://www.blocknotejs.org/pricing) and would appreciate if you could look into this sooner than later 💖

</pr_description>

Because working with row and column-spanning cells is not quite\n// trivial, this code builds up a descriptive structure for a given\n// table node. The structures are cached with the (persistent) table\n// nodes as key, so that they only have to be recomputed when the\n// content of the table changes.\n//\n// This does mean that they have to store table-relative, not\n// document-relative positions. So code that uses them will typically\n// compute the start position of the table and offset positions passed\n// to or gotten from this structure by that amount.\nimport type { Attrs, Node } from 'prosemirror-model';\n\nimport type { CellAttrs } from './util';\n\n/**\n * @public\n */\nexport type ColWidths = number[];\n\n/**\n * @public\n */\nexport type Problem =\n  | {\n      type: 'colwidth mismatch';\n      pos: number;\n      colwidth: ColWidths;\n    }\n  | {\n      type: 'collision';\n      pos: number;\n      row: number;\n      n: number;\n    }\n  | {\n      type: 'missing';\n      row: number;\n      n: number;\n    }\n  | {\n      type: 'overlong_rowspan';\n      pos: number;\n      n: number;\n    }\n  | {\n      type: 'zero_sized';\n    };\n\nlet readFromCache: (key: Node) => TableMap | undefined;\nlet addToCache: (key: Node, value: TableMap) => TableMap;\n\n// Prefer using a weak map to cache table maps. Fall back on a\n// fixed-size cache if that's not supported.\nif (typeof WeakMap != 'undefined') {\n  let cache = new WeakMap<Node, TableMap>();\n  readFromCache = (key) => cache.get(key);\n  addToCache = (key, value) => {\n    cache.set(key, value);\n    return value;\n  };\n} else {\n  const cache: (Node | TableMap)[] = [];\n  const cacheSize = 10;\n  let cachePos = 0;\n  readFromCache = (key) => {\n    for (let i = 0; i < cache.length; i += 2)\n      if (cache[i] == key) return cache[i + 1] as TableMap;\n  };\n  addToCache = (key, value) => {\n    if (cachePos == cacheSize) cachePos = 0;\n    cache[cachePos++] = key;\n    return (cache[cachePos++] = value);\n  };\n}\n\n/**\n * @public\n */\nexport interface Rect {\n  left: number;\n  top: number;\n  right: number;\n  bottom: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * A table map describes the structure of a given table. To avoid\n * recomputing them all the time, they are cached per table node. To\n * be able to do that, positions saved in the map are relative to the\n * start of the table, rather than the start of the document.\n *\n * @public\n */\nexport class TableMap {\n  constructor(\n    /**\n     * The number of columns\n     */\n    public width: number,\n    /**\n     * The number of rows\n     */\n    public height: number,\n    /**\n     * A width * height array with the start position of\n     * the cell covering that part of the table in each slot\n     */\n    public map: number[],\n    /**\n     * An optional array of problems (cell overlap or non-rectangular\n     * shape) for the table, used by the table normalizer.\n     */\n    public problems: Problem[] | null,\n  ) {}\n\n  // Find the dimensions of the cell at the given position.\n  findCell(pos: number): Rect {\n    for (let i = 0; i < this.map.length; i++) {\n      const curPos = this.map[i];\n      if (curPos != pos) continue;\n\n      const left = i % this.width;\n      const top = (i / this.width) | 0;\n      let right = left + 1;\n      let bottom = top + 1;\n\n      for (let j = 1; right < this.width && this.map[i + j] == curPos; j++) {\n        right++;\n      }\n      for (\n        let j = 1;\n        bottom < this.height && this.map[i + this.width * j] == curPos;\n        j++\n      ) {\n        bottom++;\n      }\n\n      return { left, top, right, bottom };\n    }\n    throw new RangeError(`No cell with offset ${pos} found`);\n  }\n\n  // Find the left side of the cell at the given position.\n  colCount(pos: number): number {\n    for (let i = 0; i < this.map.length; i++) {\n      if (this.map[i] == pos) {\n        return i % this.width;\n      }\n    }\n    throw new RangeError(`No cell with offset ${pos} found`);\n  }\n\n  // Find the next cell in the given direction, starting from the cell\n  // at `pos`, if any.\n  nextCell(pos: number, axis: 'horiz' | 'vert', dir: number): null | number {\n    const { left, right, top, bottom } = this.findCell(pos);\n    if (axis == 'horiz') {\n      if (dir < 0 ? left == 0 : right == this.width) return null;\n      return this.map[top * this.width + (dir < 0 ? left - 1 : right)];\n    } else {\n      if (dir < 0 ? top == 0 : bottom == this.height) return null;\n      return this.map[left + this.width * (dir < 0 ? top - 1 : bottom)];\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Get the rectangle spanning the two given cells.\n  rectBetween(a: number, b: number): Rect {\n    const {\n      left: leftA,\n      right: rightA,\n      top: topA,\n      bottom: bottomA,\n    } = this.findCell(a);\n    const {\n      left: leftB,\n      right: rightB,\n      top: topB,\n      bottom: bottomB,\n    } = this.findCell(b);\n    return {\n      left: Math.min(leftA, leftB),\n      top: Math.min(topA, topB),\n      right: Math.max(rightA, rightB),\n      bottom: Math.max(bottomA, bottomB),\n    };\n  }\n\n  // Return the position of all cells that have the top left corner in\n  // the given rectangle.\n  cellsInRect(rect: Rect): number[] {\n    const result: number[] = [];\n    const seen: Record<number, boolean> = {};\n    for (let row = rect.top; row < rect.bottom; row++) {\n      for (let col = rect.left; col < rect.right; col++) {\n        const index = row * this.width + col;\n        const pos = this.map[index];\n\n        if (seen[pos]) continue;\n        seen[pos] = true;\n\n        if (\n          (col == rect.left && col && this.map[index - 1] == pos) ||\n          (row == rect.top && row && this.map[index - this.width] == pos)\n        ) {\n          continue;\n        }\n        result.push(pos);\n      }\n    }\n    return result;\n  }\n\n  // Return the position at which the cell at the given row and column\n  // starts, or would start, if a cell started there.\n  positionAt(row: number, col: number, table: Node): number {\n    for (let i = 0, rowStart = 0; ; i++) {\n      const rowEnd = rowStart + table.child(i).nodeSize;\n      if (i == row) {\n        let index = col + row * this.width;\n        const rowEndIndex = (row + 1) * this.width;\n        // Skip past cells from previous rows (via rowspan)\n        while (index < rowEndIndex && this.map[index] < rowStart) index++;\n        return index == rowEndIndex ? rowEnd - 1 : this.map[index];\n      }\n      rowStart = rowEnd;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Find the table map for the given table node.\n  static get(table: Node): TableMap {\n    return readFromCache(table) || addToCache(table, computeMap(table));\n  }\n}\n\n// Compute a table map.\nfunction computeMap(table: Node): TableMap {\n  if (table.type.spec.tableRole != 'table')\n    throw new RangeError('Not a table node: ' + table.type.name);\n  const width = findWidth(table),\n    height = table.childCount;\n  const map = [];\n  let mapPos = 0;\n  let problems: Problem[] | null = null;\n  const colWidths: ColWidths = [];\n  for (let i = 0, e = width * height; i < e; i++) map[i] = 0;\n\n  for (let row = 0, pos = 0; row < height; row++) {\n    const rowNode = table.child(row);\n    pos++;\n    for (let i = 0; ; i++) {\n      while (mapPos < map.length && map[mapPos] != 0) mapPos++;\n      if (i == rowNode.childCount) break;\n      const cellNode = rowNode.child(i);\n      const { colspan, rowspan, colwidth } = cellNode.attrs;\n      for (let h = 0; h < rowspan; h++) {\n        if (h + row >= height) {\n          (problems || (problems = [])).push({\n            type: 'overlong_rowspan',\n            pos,\n            n: rowspan - h,\n          });\n          break;\n        }\n        const start = mapPos + h * width;\n        for (let w = 0; w < colspan; w++) {\n          if (map[start + w] == 0) map[start + w] = pos;\n          else\n            (problems || (problems = [])).push({\n              type: 'collision',\n              row,\n              pos,\n              n: colspan - w,\n            });\n          const colW = colwidth && colwidth[w];\n          if (colW) {\n            const widthIndex = ((start + w) % width) * 2,\n              prev = colWidths[widthIndex];\n            if (\n              prev == null ||\n              (prev != colW && colWidths[widthIndex + 1] == 1)\n            ) {\n              colWidths[widthIndex] = colW;\n              colWidths[widthIndex + 1] = 1;\n            } else if (prev == colW) {\n              colWidths[widthIndex + 1]++;\n expectedPos) if (map[mapPos++] == 0) missing++;\n    if (missing)\n      (problems || (problems = [])).push({ type: 'missing', row, n: missing });\n    pos++;\n  }\n\n  if (width === 0 || height === widths, but whose widths disagree\n  // between rows, fix up the cells whose width doesn't match the\n  // computed one.\n  for (let i = 0; !badWidths && i < colWidths.length; i += 2)\n    if cell.attrs.rowspan > row) rowWidth += cell.attrs.colspan;\n        }\n      }\n    for (let i = 0; i < rowNode.childCount; i++) {\n      const cell = rowNode.child(i);\n      rowWidth += cell.attrs.colspan;\n      if (cell.attrs.rowspan > 1) hasRowSpan = true;\n    }\n    if (width == -1) width = rowWidth;\n    else if (width != rowWidth) width = Math.max(width, rowWidth);\n  }\n tableStart,\n      $headCell.pos - tableStart,\n    );\n\n    const doc = $anchorCell.node(0);\n    const cells = map\n      .cellsInRect(rect)\n      .filter((p) => p != $headCell.pos - tableStart);\n    // Make the head cell the first range, so that it counts as the\n    // primary part of the selection\n    cells.unshift($headCell.pos - cellRect.left;\n        const extraRight = cellRect.right - rect.right;\n\n        if (extraLeft > 0 || extraRight > 0) {\n          let attrs = cell.attrs as CellAttrs;\n          if (extraLeft > 0) {\n            attrs = removeColSpan(attrs, 0, extraLeft);\n          }\n          if (extraRight > 0) {\n            attrs = removeColSpan(\n              attrs,\n              attrs.colspan - Uses the problems\n// reported by `TableMap`.\n\nimport type { Node } from 'prosemirror-model';\nimport type { EditorState, Transaction } from 'prosemirror-state';\nimport { PluginKey } from 'prosemirror-state';\n\nimport type { TableRole } from './schema';\nimport { tableNodeTypes } from './schema';\nimport { TableMap } from './tablemap';\nimport type { CellAttrs } from './util';\nimport { removeColSpan } from './util';\n\n/**\n * @public\n */\nexport const fixTablesKey = new PluginKey<{ fixTables: boolean }>('fix-tables');\n\n/**\n * Helper for iterating through the nodes in a document that changed\n * compared to the given previous document. Useful for avoiding\n * duplicate work on each transaction.\n *\n * @public\n */\nfunction changedDescendants(\n  old: Node,\n  cur: Node,\n  offset: number,\n  f: (node: Node, pos: number) => void,\n): void {\n  const oldSize = old.childCount,\n    curSize = cur.childCount;\n  outer: for (let i = 0, j = 0; i < curSize; i++) {\n    const child = cur.child(i);\n    for (let scan = j, e = Math.min(oldSize, i + 3); scan < e; scan++) {\n      if (old.child(scan) == child) {\n        j = scan + 1;\n        offset += child.nodeSize;\n        continue outer;\n      }\n    }\n    f(child, offset);\n    if (j < oldSize && old.child(j).sameMarkup(child))\n      changedDescendants(old.child(j), child, offset + 1, f);\n    else child.nodesBetween(0, child.content.size, f, offset + 1);\n    offset += child.nodeSize;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Inspect all tables in the given state's document and return a\n * transaction that fixes them, if necessary. Will append to the transaction\n// it was given, if non-null, or create a new one if necessary.\nexport function fixTable(\n  state: EditorState,\n  table: Node,\n  tablePos: number,\n  tr: Transaction | undefined,\n): Transaction | undefined {\n  const map = TableMap.get(table);\n  if (!map.problems) return tr;\n  if (!tr) tr = state.tr;\n\n  // Track which rows we must add cells to, so that we can adjust that\n  // when fixing collisions.\n  const mustAdd: number[] = [];\n  for (let i = 0; i < map.height; i++) mustAdd.push(0);\n  for (let i = 0; i < map.problems.length; i++) {\n    const prob = map.problems[i];\n    if (prob.type == 'collision') {\n      const cell = table.nodeAt(prob.pos);\n      if (!cell) continue;\n      const attrs = cell.attrs as CellAttrs;\n      for (let j = 0; j < attrs.rowspan; j++) mustAdd[prob.row + j] += prob.n;\n      tr.setNodeMarkup(\n        tr.mapping.map(tablePos + 1 + prob.pos),\n        null,\n        removeColSpan(attrs, attrs.colspan - prob.n, prob.n),\n      );\n    } else if (prob.type == 'missing') {\n      mustAdd[prob.row] += prob.n;\n    } else if (prob.type == 'overlong_rowspan') {\n      const cell = table.nodeAt(prob.pos);\n      if (!cell) continue;\n      tr.setNodeMarkup(tr.mapping.map(tablePos + 1 + prob.pos), null, {\n        ...cell.attrs,\n        rowspan: cell.attrs.rowspan - prob.n,\n      });\n    } else if (prob.type == 'colwidth mismatch') {\n      const cell = table.nodeAt(prob.pos);\n      if (!cell) continue;\n      tr.setNodeMarkup(tr.mapping.map(tablePos + 1 + prob.pos), null, {\n        ...cell.attrs,\n        colwidth: prob.colwidth,\n      });\n    } else if (prob.type == 'zero_sized') {\n      const pos = tr.mapping.map(tablePos);\n      tr.delete(pos, pos + table.nodeSize);\n    }\n  }\n  let first, last;\n  for (let i = 0; i < mustAdd.length; i++)\n    if (mustAdd[i]) {\n      if (first == null) first = i;\n      last = i;\n    }\n  // Add the necessary cells, using a heuristic for whether to add the\n  // cells at the start or end of the rows (if it looks like a 'bite'\n  // was taken out of the table, add cells at the start of the row\n  // after the bite.      1	import { Node } from "@tiptap/core";
     2	
     3	import { createColumnResizeExtension } from "../extensions/ColumnResize/ColumnResizeExtension.js";
     4	
     5	export const Column = Node.create({
     6	  name: "column",
     7	  group: "bnBlock childContainer",
     8	  // A block always contains content, and optionally a blockGroup which contains nested blocks
     9	  content: "blockContainer+",
    10	  priority: 40,
    11	  defining: true,
    12	  marks: "deletion insertion modification",
    13	  addAttributes() {
    14	    return {
    15	      width: {
    16	        // Why does each column have a default width of 1, i.e. 100%? Because
    17	        // when creating a new column, we want to make sure that existing
    18	        // column widths are preserved, while the new one also has a sensible
    19	        // width. If we'd set it so all column widths must add up to 100%
    20	        // instead, then each time a new column is created, we'd have to assign
    21	        // it a width depending on the total number of columns and also adjust
    22	        // the widths of the other columns. The same can be said for using px
    23	        // instead of percent widths and making them add to the editor width. So
    24	        // using this method is both simpler and computationally cheaper. This
    25	        // is possible because we can set the `flex-grow` property to the width
    26	        // value, which handles all the resizing for us, instead of manually
    27	        // having to set the `width` property of each column.
    28	        default: 1,
    29	        parseHTML: (element) => {
    30	          const attr = element.getAttribute("data-width");
    31	          if (attr === null) {
    32	            return null;
    33	          }
    34	
    35	          const parsed = parseFloat(attr);
    36	          if (isFinite(parsed)) {
    37	            return parsed;
    38	          }
    39	
    40	          return null;
    41	        },
    42	        renderHTML: (attributes) => {
    43	          return {
    44	            "data-width": (attributes.width as number).toString(),
    45	            style: `flex-grow: ${attributes.width as number};`,
    46	          };
    47	        },
    48	      },
    49	    };
    50	  },
    51	
    52	  parseHTML() {
    53	    return [
    54	      {
    55	        tag: "div",
    56	        getAttrs: (element) => {
    57	          if (typeof element === "string") {
    58	            return false;
    59	          }
    60	
    61	          if (element.getAttribute("data-node-type") === this.name) {
    62	            return {};
    63	          }
    64	
    65	          return false;
    66	        },
    67	      },
    68	    ];
    69	  },
    70	
    71	  renderHTML({ HTMLAttributes }) {
    72	    const column = document.createElement("div");
    73	    column.className = "bn-block-column";
    74	    column.setAttribute("data-node-type", this.name);
    75	    for (const [attribute, value] of Object.entries(HTMLAttributes)) {
    76	      column.setAttribute(attribute, value as any); // TODO as any
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    return {
    80	      dom: column,
    81	      contentDOM: column,
    82	    };
    83	  },
    84	
    85	  addExtensions() {
    86	    return [createColumnResizeExtension(this.options.editor)];
    87	  },
    88	});
    89

   351	
   352	    const handleDelete = () =>
   353	      this.editor.commands.first(({ chain, commands }) => [
   354	        // Deletes the selection if it's not empty.
   355	        () => commands.deleteSelection(),
   356	        // Deletes the first child block and un-nests its children, if the
   357	        // selection is empty and at the end of the current block. If both the
   358	        // parent and child blocks have inline content, the child block's
   359	        // content is appended to the parent's. The child block's own children
   360	        // are unindented before it's deleted.
   361	        () =>
   362	          commands.command(({ state }) => {
   363	            const blockInfo = getBlockInfoFromSelection(state);
   364	            if (!blockInfo.isBlockContainer || !blockInfo.childContainer) {
   365	              return false;
   366	            }
   367	            const { blockContent, childContainer } = blockInfo;
   368	
   369	            const selectionAtBlockEnd =
   370	              state.selection.from === blockContent.afterPos - 1;
   371	            const selectionEmpty = state.selection.empty;
   372	
   373	            const firstChildBlockInfo = getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(
   374	              state.doc.resolve(childContainer.beforePos + 1),
   375	            );
   376	            if (!firstChildBlockInfo.isBlockContainer) {
   377	              return false;
   378	            }
   379	
   380	            if (selectionAtBlockEnd && selectionEmpty) {
   381	              const firstChildBlockContent =
   382	                firstChildBlockInfo.blockContent.node;
   383	              const firstChildBlockHasInlineContent =
   384	                firstChildBlockContent.type.spec.content === "inline*";
   385	              const blockHasInlineContent =
   386	                blockContent.node.type.spec.content === "inline*";
   387	
   388	              return (
   389	                chain()
   390	                  // Un-nests child block's children if necessary.
   391	                  .insertContentAt(
   392	                    firstChildBlockInfo.bnBlock.afterPos,
   393	                    firstChildBlockInfo.childContainer?.node.content ||
   394	                      Fragment.empty,
   395	                  )
   396	                  .deleteRange(
   397	                    // Deletes whole child container if there's only one child.
   398	                    childContainer.node.childCount === 1
   399	                      ? {
   400	                          from: childContainer.beforePos,
   401	                          to: childContainer.afterPos,
   402	                        }
   403	                      : {
   404	                          from: firstChildBlockInfo.bnBlock.beforePos,
   405	                          to: firstChildBlockInfo.bnBlock.afterPos,
   406	                        },
   407	                  )
   408	                  // Appends inline content from child block if possible.
   409	                  .insertContentAt(
   410	                    state.selection.from,
   411	                    firstChildBlockHasInlineContent && blockHasInlineContent
   412	                      ? firstChildBlockContent.content
   413	                      : null,
   414	                  )
   415	                  .setTextSelection(state.selection.from)
   416	                  .scrollIntoView()
   417	                  .run()
   418	              );
   419	            }
   420	
   421	            return false;
   422	          }),
   423	        // Merges block with the next one (at the same nesting level or lower),
   424	        // if one exists, the block has no children, and the selection is at the
   425	        // end of the block.
   426	        () =>
   427	          commands.command(({ state }) => {
   428	            const blockInfo = getBlockInfoFromSelection(state);
   429	            if (!blockInfo.isBlockContainer) {
   430	              return false;

     2	import { EditorState } from "prosemirror-state";
     3	
     4	import {
     5	  BlockInfo,
     6	  getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos,
     7	} from "../../../getBlockInfoFromPos.js";
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * Returns the block info from the parent block
    11	 * or undefined if we're at the root
    12	 */
    13	export const getParentBlockInfo = (
    14	  doc: Node,
    15	  beforePos: number,
    16	): BlockInfo | undefined => {
    17	  const $pos = doc.resolve(beforePos);
    18	  const depth = $pos.depth - 1;
    19	
    20	  if (depth < 1) {
    21	    return undefined;
    22	  }
    23	
    24	  const parentBeforePos = $pos.before(depth);
    25	  const parentNode = doc.resolve(parentBeforePos).nodeAfter;
    26	
    27	  if (!parentNode) {
    28	    return undefined;
    29	  }
    30	
    31	  if (!parentNode.type.spec.group?.includes("bnBlock")) {
    32	    return getParentBlockInfo(doc, parentBeforePos);
    33	  }
    34	
    35	  const parentBlockInfo = getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(
    36	    doc.resolve(parentBeforePos),
    37	  );
    38	
    39	  return parentBlockInfo;
    40	};
    41	
    42	/**
    43	 * Returns the block info from the sibling block before (above) the given block,
    44	 * or undefined if the given block is the first sibling.
    45	 */
    46	export const getPrevBlockInfo = (doc: Node, beforePos: number) => {
    47	  const $pos = doc.resolve(beforePos);
    48	
    49	  const indexInParent = $pos.index();
    50	
    51	  if (indexInParent === 0) {
    52	    return undefined;
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  const prevBlockBeforePos = $pos.posAtIndex(indexInParent - 1);
    56	
    57	  const prevBlockInfo = getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(
    58	    doc.resolve(prevBlockBeforePos),
    59	  );
    60	  return prevBlockInfo;
    61	};
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Returns the block info from the sibling block after (below) the given block,
    65	 * or undefined if the given block is the last sibling.
    66	 */
    67	export const getNextBlockInfo = (doc: Node, beforePos: number) => {
    68	  const $pos = doc.resolve(beforePos);
    69	
    70	  const indexInParent = $pos.index();
    71	
    72	  if (indexInParent === $pos.node().childCount - 1) {
    73	    return undefined;
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  const nextBlockBeforePos = $pos.posAtIndex(indexInParent + 1);
    77	
    78	  const nextBlockInfo = getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(
    79	    doc.resolve(nextBlockBeforePos),
    80	  );
    81	  return nextBlockInfo;
    82	};
    83	
    84	/**
    85	 * If a block has children like this:
    86	 * A
    87	 * - B
    88	 * - C
    89	 * -- D
    90	 *
    91	 * Then the bottom nested block returned is D.
    92	 */
    93	export const getBottomNestedBlockInfo = (doc: Node, blockInfo: BlockInfo) => {
    94	  while (blockInfo.childContainer) {
    95	    const group = blockInfo.childContainer.node;
    96	
    97	    const newPos = doc
    98	      .resolve(blockInfo.childContainer.beforePos + 1)
    99	      .posAtIndex(group.childCount - 1);
   100	    blockInfo = getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(doc.resolve(newPos));
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  return blockInfo;
   104	};
   105	
   106	const canMerge = (prevBlockInfo: BlockInfo, nextBlockInfo: BlockInfo) => {
   107	  return (
   108	    prevBlockInfo.isBlockContainer &&
   109	    prevBlockInfo.blockContent.node.type.spec.content === "inline*" &&
   110	    prevBlockInfo.blockContent.node.childCount > 0 &&
   111	    nextBlockInfo.isBlockContainer &&
   112	    nextBlockInfo.blockContent.node.type.spec.content === "inline*"
   113	  );
   114	};

     1	import { Node, ResolvedPos } from "prosemirror-model";
     2	import { EditorState, Transaction } from "prosemirror-state";
     3	
     4	type SingleBlockInfo = {
     5	  node: Node;
     6	  beforePos: number;
     7	  afterPos: number;
     8	};
     9	
    10	export type BlockInfo = {
    11	  /**
    12	   * The outer node that represents a BlockNote block. This is the node that has the ID.
    13	   * Most of the time, this will be a blockContainer node, but it could also be a Column or ColumnList
    14	   */
    15	  bnBlock: SingleBlockInfo;
    16	  /**
    17	   * The type of BlockNote block that this node represents.
    18	   * When dealing with a blockContainer, this is retrieved from the blockContent node, otherwise it's retrieved from the bnBlock node.
    19	   */
    20	  blockNoteType: string;
    21	} & (
    22	  | {
    23	      // In case we're not dealing with a BlockContainer, we're dealing with a "wrapper node" (like a Column or ColumnList), so it will always have children
    24	
    25	      /**
    26	       * The Prosemirror node that holds block.children. For non-blockContainer, this node will be the same as bnBlock.
    27	       */
    28	      childContainer: SingleBlockInfo;
    29	      isBlockContainer: false;
    30	    }
    31	  | {
    32	      /**
    33	       * The Prosemirror node that holds block.children. For blockContainers, this is the blockGroup node, if it exists.
    34	       */
    35	      childContainer?: SingleBlockInfo;
    36	      /**
    37	       * The Prosemirror node that wraps block.content and has most of the props
    38	       */
    39	      blockContent: SingleBlockInfo;
    40	      /**
    41	       * Whether bnBlock is a blockContainer node
    42	       */
    43	      isBlockContainer: true;
    44	    }
    45	);
    46	
    47	/**
    48	 * Retrieves the position just before the nearest block node in a ProseMirror
    49	 * doc, relative to a position. If the position is within a block node or its
    50	 * descendants, the position just before it is returned. If the position is not
    51	 * within a block node or its descendants, the position just before the next
    52	 * closest block node is returned. If the position is beyond the last block, the
    53	 * position just before the last block is returned.
    54	 * @param doc The ProseMirror doc.
    55	 * @param pos An integer position in the document.
    56	 * @returns The position just before the nearest blockContainer node.
    57	 */
    58	export function getNearestBlockPos(doc: Node, pos: number) {
    59	  const $pos = doc.resolve(pos);
    60	
    61	  // Checks if the position provided is already just before a block node, in
    62	  // which case we return the position.
    63	  if ($pos.nodeAfter && $pos.nodeAfter.type.isInGroup("bnBlock")) {
    64	    return {
    65	      posBeforeNode: $pos.pos,
    66	      node: $pos.nodeAfter,
    67	    };
    68	  }
    69	
    70	  // Checks the node containing the position and its ancestors until a
    71	  // block node is found and returned.
    72	  let depth = $pos.depth;
    73	  let node = $pos.node(depth);
    74	  while (depth > 0) {
    75	    if (node.type.isInGroup("bnBlock")) {
    76	      return {
    77	        posBeforeNode: $pos.before(depth),
    78	        node: node,
    79	      };
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    depth--;
    83	    node = $pos.node(depth);
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  // If the position doesn't lie within a block node, we instead find the
    87	  // position of the next closest one. If the position is beyond the last block,
    88	  // we return the position of the last block. While running `doc.descendants`
    89	  // is expensive, this case should be very rarely triggered. However, it's
    90	  // possible for the position to sometimes be beyond the last block node. This
    91	  // is a problem specifically when using the collaboration plugin.
    92	  const allBlockContainerPositions: number[] = [];
    93	  doc.descendants((node, pos) => {
    94	    if (node.type.isInGroup("bnBlock")) {
    95	      allBlockContainerPositions.push(pos);
    96	    }
    97	  });
    98	
    99	  // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   100	  console.warn(`Position ${pos} is not within a blockContainer node.`);
   101	
   102	  const resolvedPos = doc.resolve(
   103	    allBlockContainerPositions.find((position) => position >= pos) ||
   104	      allBlockContainerPositions[allBlockContainerPositions.length - 1],
   105	  );
   106	  return {
   107	    posBeforeNode: resolvedPos.pos,
   108	    node: resolvedPos.nodeAfter!,
   109	  };
   110	}
   111	
   112	/**
   113	 * Gets information regarding the ProseMirror nodes that make up a block in a
   114	 * BlockNote document. This includes the main `blockContainer` node, the
   115	 * `blockContent` node with the block's main body, and the optional `blockGroup`
   116	 * node which contains the block's children. As well as the nodes, also returns
   117	 * the ProseMirror positions just before & after each node.
   118	 * @param node The main `blockContainer` node that the block information should
   119	 * be retrieved from,
   120	 * @param bnBlockBeforePosOffset the position just before the
   121	 * `blockContainer` node in the document.
   122	 */
   123	export function getBlockInfoWithManualOffset(
   124	  node: Node,
   125	  bnBlockBeforePosOffset: number,
   126	): BlockInfo {
   127	  if (!node.type.isInGroup("bnBlock")) {
   128	    throw new Error(
   129	      `Attempted to get bnBlock node at position but found node of different type ${node.type.name}`,
   130	    );
   131	  }
   132	
   133	  const bnBlockNode = node;
   134	  const bnBlockBeforePos = bnBlockBeforePosOffset;
   135	  const bnBlockAfterPos = bnBlockBeforePos + bnBlockNode.nodeSize;
   136	
   137	  const bnBlock: SingleBlockInfo = {
   138	    node: bnBlockNode,
   139	    beforePos: bnBlockBeforePos,
   140	    afterPos: bnBlockAfterPos,
   141	  };
   142	
   143	  if (bnBlockNode.type.name === "blockContainer") {
   144	    let blockContent: SingleBlockInfo | undefined;
   145	    let blockGroup: SingleBlockInfo | undefined;
   146	
   147	    bnBlockNode.forEach((node, offset) => {
   148	      if (node.type.spec.group === "blockContent") {
   149	        // console.log(beforePos, offset);
   150	        const blockContentNode = node;
   151	        const blockContentBeforePos = bnBlockBeforePos + offset + 1;
   152	        const blockContentAfterPos = blockContentBeforePos + node.nodeSize;
   153	
   154	        blockContent = {
   155	          node: blockContentNode,
   156	          beforePos: blockContentBeforePos,
   157	          afterPos: blockContentAfterPos,
   158	        };
   159	      } else if (node.type.name === "blockGroup") {
   160	        const blockGroupNode = node;
   161	        const blockGroupBeforePos = bnBlockBeforePos + offset + 1;
   162	        const blockGroupAfterPos = blockGroupBeforePos + node.nodeSize;
   163	
   164	        blockGroup = {
   165	          node: blockGroupNode,
   166	          beforePos: blockGroupBeforePos,
   167	          afterPos: blockGroupAfterPos,
   168	        };
   169	      }
   170	    });
   171	
   172	    if (!blockContent) {
   173	      throw new Error(
   174	        `blockContainer node does not contain a blockContent node in its children: ${bnBlockNode}`,
   175	      );
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    return {
   179	      isBlockContainer: true,
   180	      bnBlock,
   181	      blockContent,
   182	      childContainer: blockGroup,
   183	      blockNoteType: blockContent.node.type.name,
   184	    };
   185	  } else {
   186	    if (!bnBlock.node.type.isInGroup("childContainer")) {
   187	      throw new Error(
   188	        `bnBlock node is not in the childContainer group: ${bnBlock.node}`,
   189	      );
   190	    }
   191	
   192	    return {
   193	      isBlockContainer: false,
   194	      bnBlock: bnBlock,
   195	      childContainer: bnBlock,
   196	      blockNoteType: bnBlock.node.type.name,
   197	    };
   198	  }
   199	}
   200	
   201	/**
   202	 * Gets information regarding the ProseMirror nodes that make up a block in a
   203	 * BlockNote document. This includes the main `blockContainer` node, the
   204	 * `blockContent` node with the block's main body, and the optional `blockGroup`
   205	 * node which contains the block's children. As well as the nodes, also returns
   206	 * the ProseMirror positions just before & after each node.
   207	 * @param posInfo An object with the main `blockContainer` node that the block
   208	 * information should be retrieved from, and the position just before it in the
   209	 * document.
   210	 */
   211	export function getBlockInfo(posInfo: { posBeforeNode: number; node: Node }) {
   212	  return getBlockInfoWithManualOffset(posInfo.node, posInfo.posBeforeNode);
   213	}
   214	
   215	/**
   216	 * Gets information regarding the ProseMirror nodes that make up a block from a
   217	 * resolved position just before the `blockContainer` node in the document that
   218	 * corresponds to it.
   219	 * @param resolvedPos The resolved position just before the `blockContainer`
   220	 * node.
   221	 */
   222	export function getBlockInfoFromResolvedPos(resolvedPos: ResolvedPos) {
   223	  if (!resolvedPos.nodeAfter) {
   224	    throw new Error(
   225	      `Attempted to get blockContainer node at position ${resolvedPos.pos} but a node at this position does not exist`,
   226	    );
   227	  }
   228	  return getBlockInfoWithManualOffset(resolvedPos.nodeAfter, resolvedPos.pos);
   229	}
   230	
   231	/**
   232	 * Gets information regarding the ProseMirror nodes that make up a block. The
   233	 * block chosen is the one currently containing the current ProseMirror
   234	 * selection.
   235	 * @param state The ProseMirror editor state.
   236	 */
   237	export function getBlockInfoFromSelection(state: EditorState) {
   238	  const posInfo = getNearestBlockPos(state.doc, state.selection.anchor);
   239	
   240	  return getBlockInfo(posInfo);
   241	}
   242	
   243	/**
   244	 * Gets information regarding the ProseMirror nodes that make up a block. The
   245	 * block chosen is the one currently containing the current ProseMirror
   246	 * selection.
   247	 * @param tr The ProseMirror transaction.
   248	 */
   249	export function getBlockInfoFromTransaction(tr: Transaction) {
   250	  const posInfo = getNearestBlockPos(tr.doc, tr.selection.anchor);
   251	
   252	  return getBlockInfo(posInfo);
   253	}

     1	import { Command, Transaction } from "prosemirror-state";
     2	import type { YUndoExtension } from "../../extensions/Collaboration/YUndo.js";
     3	import type { HistoryExtension } from "../../extensions/History/History.js";
     4	import { BlockNoteEditor } from "../BlockNoteEditor.js";
     5	
     6	export class StateManager {
     7	  constructor(private editor: BlockNoteEditor<any, any, any>) {}
     8	
     9	  /**
    10	   * Stores the currently active transaction, which is the accumulated transaction from all {@link dispatch} calls during a {@link transact} calls
    11	   */
    12	  private activeTransaction: Transaction | null = null;
    13	
    14	  /**
    15	   * For any command that can be executed, you can check if it can be executed by calling `editor.can(command)`.
    16	   * @example
    17	   * ```ts
    18	   * if (editor.can(editor.undo)) {
    19	   *   // show button
    20	   * } else {
    21	   *   // hide button
    22	   * }
    23	   */
    24	  public can(cb: () => boolean) {
    25	    try {
    26	      this.isInCan = true;
    27	      return cb();
    28	    } finally {
    29	      this.isInCan = false;
    30	    }
    31	  }
    32	
    33	  // Flag to indicate if we're in a `can` call
    34	  private isInCan = false;
    35	
    36	  /**
    37	   * Execute a prosemirror command. This is mostly for backwards compatibility with older code.
    38	   *
    39	   * @note You should prefer the {@link transact} method when possible, as it will automatically handle the dispatching of the transaction and work across blocknote transactions.
    40	   *
    41	   * @example
    42	   * ```ts
    43	   * editor.exec((state, dispatch, view) => {
    44	   *   dispatch(state.tr.insertText("Hello, world!"));
    45	   * });
    46	   * ```
    47	   */
    48	  public exec(command: Command) {
    49	    if (this.activeTransaction) {
    50	      throw new Error(
    51	        "`exec` should not be called within a `transact` call, move the `exec` call outside of the `transact` call",
    52	      );
    53	    }
    54	    if (this.isInCan) {
    55	      return this.canExec(command);
    56	    }
    57	    const state = this.prosemirrorState;
    58	    const view = this.prosemirrorView;
    59	    const dispatch = (tr: Transaction) => this.prosemirrorView.dispatch(tr);
    60	
    61	    return command(state, dispatch, view);
    62	  }
    63	
    64	  /**
    65	   * Check if a command can be executed. A command should return `false` if it is not valid in the current state.
    66	   *
    67	   * @example
    68	   * ```ts
    69	   * if (editor.canExec(command)) {
    70	   *   // show button
    71	   * } else {
    72	   *   // hide button
    73	   * }
    74	   * ```
    75	   */
    76	  public canExec(command: Command): boolean {
    77	    if (this.activeTransaction) {
    78	      throw new Error(
    79	        "`canExec` should not be called within a `transact` call, move the `canExec` call outside of the `transact` call",
    80	      );
    81	    }
    82	    const state = this.prosemirrorState;
    83	    const view = this.prosemirrorView;
    84	
    85	    return command(state, undefined, view);
    86	  }
    87	
    88	  /**
    89	   * Execute a function within a "blocknote transaction".
    90	   * All changes to the editor within the transaction will be grouped together, so that
    91	   * we can dispatch them as a single operation (thus creating only a single undo step)
    92	   *
    93	   * @note There is no need to dispatch the transaction, as it will be automatically dispatched when the callback is complete.
    94	   *
    95	   * @example
    96	   * ```ts
    97	   * // All changes to the editor will be grouped together
    98	   * editor.transact((tr) => {
    99	   *   tr.insertText("Hello, world!");
   100	   * // These two operations will be grouped together in a single undo step
   101	   *   editor.transact((tr) => {
   102	   *     tr.insertText("Hello, world!");
   103	   *   });
   104	   * });
   105	   * ```
   106	   */
   107	  public transact<T>(
   108	    callback: (
   109	      /**
   110	       * The current active transaction, this will automatically be dispatched to the editor when the callback is complete
   111	       * If another `transact` call is made within the callback, it will be passed the same transaction as the parent call.
   112	       */
   113	      tr: Transaction,
   114	    ) => T,
   115	  ): T {
   116	    if (this.activeTransaction) {
   117	      // Already in a transaction, so we can just callback immediately
   118	      return callback(this.activeTransaction);
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    try {
   122	      // Enter transaction mode, by setting a starting transaction
   123	      this.activeTransaction = this.editor._tiptapEditor.state.tr;
   124	
   125	      // Capture all dispatch'd transactions
   126	      const result = callback(this.activeTransaction);
   127	
   128	      // Any transactions captured by the `dispatch` call will be stored in `this.activeTransaction`
   129	      const activeTr = this.activeTransaction;

   137	          activeTr.scrolledIntoView ||
   138	          activeTr.storedMarksSet ||
   139	          !activeTr.isGeneric)

    94	   */
    95	  public getSelectionBoundingBox() {
    96	    if (!this.editor.prosemirrorView) {
    97	      return undefined;
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    const { selection } = this.editor.prosemirrorState;
   101	
   102	    // support for CellSelections
   103	    const { ranges } = selection;
   104	    const from = Math.min(...ranges.map((range) => range.$from.pos));
   105	    const to = Math.max(...ranges.map((range) => range.$to.pos));
   106	
   107	    if (isNodeSelection(selection)) {
   108	      const node = this.editor.prosemirrorView.nodeDOM(from) as HTMLElement;
   109	      if (node) {
   110	        return node.getBoundingClientRect();
   111	      }
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    return posToDOMRect(
   115	      this.editor.prosemirrorView,
   116	      from,
   117	      to,
   118	    ).toJSON() as DOMRect;
   119	  }

    14	import { UnreachableCaseError } from "../../../util/typescript.js";
    15	import {
    16	  getBlockInfo,
    17	  getBlockInfoFromTransaction,
    18	} from "../../getBlockInfoFromPos.js";
    19	import { nodeToBlock } from "../../nodeConversions/nodeToBlock.js";
    20	import { getNodeById } from "../../nodeUtil.js";
    21	import { getBlockNoteSchema, getPmSchema } from "../../pmUtil.js";
    22	
    23	export function getTextCursorPosition<
    24	  BSchema extends BlockSchema,
    25	  I extends InlineContentSchema,
    26	  S extends StyleSchema,
    27	>(tr: Transaction): TextCursorPosition<BSchema, I, S> {
    28	  const { bnBlock } = getBlockInfoFromTransaction(tr);
    29	  const pmSchema = getPmSchema(tr.doc);
    30	
    31	  const resolvedPos = tr.doc.resolve(bnBlock.beforePos);
    32	  // Gets previous blockContainer node at the same nesting level, if the current node isn't the first child.
    33	  const prevNode = resolvedPos.nodeBefore;
    34	
    35	  // Gets next blockContainer node at the same nesting level, if the current node isn't the last child.
    36	  const nextNode = tr.doc.resolve(bnBlock.afterPos).nodeAfter;
    37	
    38	  // Gets parent blockContainer node, if the current node is nested.
    39	  let parentNode: Node | undefined = undefined;
    40	  if (resolvedPos.depth > 1) {
    41	    // for nodes nested in bnBlocks
    42	    parentNode = resolvedPos.node();
    43	    if (!parentNode.type.isInGroup("bnBlock")) {
    44	      // for blockGroups, we need to go one level up
    45	      parentNode = resolvedPos.node(resolvedPos.depth - 1);
    46	    }
    47	  }
    48	
    49	  return {
    50	    block: nodeToBlock(bnBlock.node, pmSchema),
    51	    prevBlock: prevNode === null ? undefined : nodeToBlock(prevNode, pmSchema),
    52	    nextBlock: nextNode === null ? undefined : nodeToBlock(nextNode, pmSchema),
    53	    parentBlock:
    54	      parentNode === undefined ? undefined : nodeToBlock(parentNode, pmSchema),
    55	  };
    56	}
    57	
    58	export function setTextCursorPosition(
    59	  tr: Transaction,
    60	  targetBlock: BlockIdentifier,
    61	  placement: "start" | "end" = "start",
    62	) {
    63	  const id = typeof targetBlock === "string" ? targetBlock : targetBlock.id;
    64	  const pmSchema = getPmSchema(tr.doc);
    65	  const schema = getBlockNoteSchema(pmSchema);
    66	
    67	  const posInfo = getNodeById(id, tr.doc);
    68	  if (!posInfo) {
    69	    throw new Error(`Block with ID ${id} not found`);
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  const info = getBlockInfo(posInfo);
    73	
    74	  const contentType: "none" | "inline" | "table" =
    75	    schema.blockSchema[info.blockNoteType]!.content;
    76	
    77	  if (info.isBlockContainer) {
    78	    const blockContent = info.blockContent;
    79	    if (contentType === "none") {
    80	      tr.setSelection(NodeSelection.create(tr.doc, blockContent.beforePos));
    81	      return;
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    if (contentType === "inline") {
    85	      if (placement === "start") {
    86	        tr.setSelection(
    87	          TextSelection.create(tr.doc, blockContent.beforePos + 1),
    88	        );
    89	      } else {
    90	        tr.setSelection(
    91	          TextSelection.create(tr.doc, blockContent.afterPos - 1),
    92	        );
    93	      }
    94	    } else if (contentType === "table") {
    95	      if (placement === "start") {
    96	        // Need to offset the position as we have to get through the `tableRow`
    97	        // and `tableCell` nodes to get to the `tableParagraph` node we want to
    98	        // set the selection in.
    99	        tr.setSelection(
   100	          TextSelection.create(tr.doc, blockContent.beforePos + 4),
   101	        );
   102	      } else {
   103	        tr.setSelection(
   104	          TextSelection.create(tr.doc, blockContent.afterPos - 4),
   105	        );
   106	      }
   107	    } else {
   108	      throw new UnreachableCaseError(contentType);
   109	    }
   110	  } else {
   111	    const child =
   112	      placement === "start"
   113	        ? info.childContainer.node.firstChild!
   114	        : info.childContainer.node.lastChild!;
   115	
   116	    setTextCursorPosition(tr, child.attrs.id, placement);
   117	  }
   118	}
   119

import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
import { BlockNoteEditor, PartialBlock } from '../packages/core/src/index.ts';
import { testEditorSchema } from '../packages/xl-multi-column/src/test/setupTestEnv.ts';

describe('repro multi-column backspace', () => {
  it('does not throw when holding backspace after a column list', () => {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    const editor = BlockNoteEditor.create({ schema: testEditorSchema });
    editor.mount(div);

    const doc: PartialBlock<any, any, any>[] = [
      {
        id: 'columns',
        type: 'columnList',
        children: [
          { id: 'col-1', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c1p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'one' }] },
          { id: 'col-2', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c2p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'two' }] },
          { id: 'col-3', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c3p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'three' }] },
        ],
      },
      { id: 'after', type: 'paragraph', content: '' },
    ];

    editor.replaceBlocks(editor.document, doc);
    editor.setTextCursorPosition('after', 'start');
    editor.transact((tr) => tr.insertText('aaa'));

    const run = () => {
      for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        editor._tiptapEditor.commands.keyboardShortcut('Backspace');
      }
    };

    expect(run).not.toThrow();
    editor._tiptapEditor.destroy();
  });
});

import type { RawCommands } from '../types.js'
import { isiOS } from '../utilities/isiOS.js'
import { isMacOS } from '../utilities/isMacOS.js'

function normalizeKeyName(name: string) {
  const parts = name.split(/-(?!$)/)
  let result = parts[parts.length - 1]

  if (result === 'Space') {
    result = ' '
  }

  let alt
  let ctrl
  let shift
  let meta

  for (let i = 0; i < parts.length - 1; i += 1) {
    const mod = parts[i]

    if (/^(cmd|meta|m)$/i.test(mod)) {
      meta = true
    } else if (/^a(lt)?$/i.test(mod)) {
      alt = true
    } else if (/^(c|ctrl|control)$/i.test(mod)) {
      ctrl = true
    } else if (/^s(hift)?$/i.test(mod)) {
      shift = true
    } else if (/^mod$/i.test(mod)) {
      if (isiOS() || isMacOS()) {
        meta = true
      } else {
        ctrl = true
      }
    } else {
      throw new Error(`Unrecognized modifier name: ${mod}`)
    }
  }

  if (alt) {
    result = `Alt-${result}`
  }

  if (ctrl) {
    result = `Ctrl-${result}`
  }

  if (meta) {
    result = `Meta-${result}`
  }

  if (shift) {
    result = `Shift-${result}`
  }

  return result
}

declare module '@tiptap/core' {
  interface Commands<ReturnType> {
    keyboardShortcut: {
      /**
       * Trigger a keyboard shortcut.
       * @param name The name of the keyboard shortcut.
       * @example editor.commands.keyboardShortcut('Mod-b')
       */
      keyboardShortcut: (name: string) => ReturnType
    }
  }
}

export const keyboardShortcut: RawCommands['keyboardShortcut'] =
  name =>
  ({ editor, view, tr, dispatch }) => {
    const keys = normalizeKeyName(name).split(/-(?!$)/)
    const key = keys.find(item => !['Alt', 'Ctrl', 'Meta', 'Shift'].includes(item))
    const event = new KeyboardEvent('keydown', {
      key: key === 'Space' ? ' ' : key,
      altKey: keys.includes('Alt'),
      ctrlKey: keys.includes('Ctrl'),
      metaKey: keys.includes('Meta'),
      shiftKey: keys.includes('Shift'),
      bubbles: true,
      cancelable: true,
    })

    const capturedTransaction = editor.captureTransaction(() => {
      view.someProp('handleKeyDown', f => f(view, event))
    })

    capturedTransaction?.steps.forEach(step => {
      const newStep = step.map(tr.mapping)

      if (newStep && dispatch) {
        tr.maybeStep(newStep)
      }
    })

    return true
  }

  public createNodeViews(): void {
    if (this.view.isDestroyed) {
      return
    }

    this.view.setProps({
      markViews: this.extensionManager.markViews,
      nodeViews: this.extensionManager.nodeViews,
    })
  }

  /**
   * Prepend class name to element.
   */
  public prependClass(): void {
    this.view.dom.className = `${this.className} ${this.view.dom.className}`
  }

  public isCapturingTransaction = false

  private capturedTransaction: Transaction | null = null

  public captureTransaction(fn: () => void) {
    this.isCapturingTransaction = true
    fn()
    this.isCapturingTransaction = false

    const tr = this.capturedTransaction

    this.capturedTransaction = null

    return tr
  }

import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
import { BlockNoteEditor, PartialBlock } from '@blocknote/core';
import { testEditorSchema } from './src/test/setupTestEnv.ts';

describe('repro multi-column backspace', () => {
  it('does not throw when holding backspace after a column list', () => {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    const editor = BlockNoteEditor.create({ schema: testEditorSchema });
    editor.mount(div);

    const doc: PartialBlock<any, any, any>[] = [
      {
        id: 'columns',
        type: 'columnList',
        children: [
          { id: 'col-1', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c1p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'one' }] },
          { id: 'col-2', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c2p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'two' }] },
          { id: 'col-3', type: 'column', children: [{ id: 'c3p', type: 'paragraph', content: 'three' }] },
        ],
      },
      { id: 'after', type: 'paragraph', content: '' },
    ];

    editor.replaceBlocks(editor.document, doc);
    editor.setTextCursorPosition('after', 'start');
    editor.transact((tr) => tr.insertText('aaa'));

    const run = () => {
      for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        const view = editor._tiptapEditor.view;
        const event = new KeyboardEvent('keydown', { key: 'Backspace', bubbles: true, cancelable: true });
        view.someProp('handleKeyDown', (f) => f(view, event));
      }
    };

    expect(run).not.toThrow();
    editor._tiptapEditor.destroy();
  });
});
EOF

import { testEditorSchema } from './src/test/setupTestEnv.ts';

function dump(editor:any, label:string){
  console.log(label, 'sel', editor._tiptapEditor.state.selection.from, editor._tiptapEditor.state.selection.to, JSON.stringify(editor.document));
}

describe('repro multi-column backspace', () => {
  it('logs', () => {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    const editor = BlockNoteEditor.create({ schema: testEditorSchema });
    editor.mount(div);
    const doc: PartialBlock<any, any, any>[] = [
      { id:'columns', type:'columnList', children:[
        { id:'col-1', type:'column', children:[{ id:'c1p', type:'paragraph', content:'one'}]},
        { id:'col-2', type:'column', children:[{ id:'c2p', type:'paragraph', content:'two'}]},
        { id:'col-3', type:'column', children:[{ id:'c3p', type:'paragraph', content:'three'}]},
      ]},
      { id:'after', type:'paragraph', content:''},
    ];
    editor.replaceBlocks(editor.document, doc);
    editor.setTextCursorPosition('after', 'start');
    editor.transact((tr) => tr.insertText('aaa'));
    dump(editor, 'start');
    for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
      const view = editor._tiptapEditor.view;
      const event = new KeyboardEvent('keydown', { key: 'Backspace', bubbles: true, cancelable: true });
      view.someProp('handleKeyDown', (f:any) => f(view, event));
      dump(editor, 'after '+i);
    }
    editor._tiptapEditor.destroy();
  });
});
EOF
